
#  Part I

```bash

sudo apt-add-repository ppa:ansible/ansible
sudo apt install -y ansible
sudo adduser ansible
sudo visudo
su - ansible
sudo apt update -y -q
sudo apt upgrade -y -q

```

#  Part II

## Connect to the hosts

```bash
  
ansible all -m ping

```

###

```bash

ubuntu | SUCCESS => {
    "ansible_facts": {
        "discovered_interpreter_python": "/usr/bin/python3"
    }, 
    "changed": false, 
    "ping": "pong"
}
jump | SUCCESS => {
    "ansible_facts": {
        "discovered_interpreter_python": "/usr/bin/python3"
    }, 
    "changed": false, 
    "ping": "pong"
}
centos | SUCCESS => {
    "ansible_facts": {
        "discovered_interpreter_python": "/usr/bin/python"
    }, 
    "changed": false, 
    "ping": "pong"

```

## Print out host names and IP

```bash
	
ansible all -m shell -a 'hostname && hostname -I'

```

###

```bash

jump | CHANGED | rc=0 >>
bastion
10.0.2.15 192.168.10.40 10.20.30.10 

ubuntu | CHANGED | rc=0 >>
ubuntu16
10.0.2.15 10.20.30.20 

centos | CHANGED | rc=0 >>
centos7
10.0.2.15 10.20.30.21 

```

## Upgrade packages

```bash

ansible ubuntu_hosts -m shell -a "apt upgrade -y -q" -b

```
